             </span>

               <article class="post hentry" id="5175970883298278523" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting">
                <h1 class="post-title entry-title" itemprop="name headline">
                 <a href="http://www.tricksworldzz.in/2015/04/tata-sky-introduces-worlds-initial.html" itemprop="url">
                  Tata Sky introduces the worlds initial Daily Recharge voucher at Rs. 8
                 </a>
                </h1>
                <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-5175970883298278523" itemprop="description articleBody">
                 <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                  <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-A-xobVZOns4/VSajBZQQTOI/AAAAAAAADKs/mmTgQBRZXZU/s1600/tata-sky-rs8-tricksworldzz.in.png" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                   <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                    <img border="0" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-A-xobVZOns4/VSajBZQQTOI/AAAAAAAADKs/mmTgQBRZXZU/s1600/tata-sky-rs8-tricksworldzz.in.png"/>
                   </span>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                  <br/>
                 </span>
                 <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                  In one more initial, Tata Sky, introduces the primary ever Daily Recharge, voucher empowering subscribers to pay just for the times they watched TV. This pioneering construct permits a minimum recharge price beginning at Rs.8/-, creating it the littlest denomination of recharge voucher within the tv viewing sector globally.
                 </span>
                 <br/>
                 <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                  <br/>
                 </span>
                 <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                  This innovation by Tata Sky puts the subscriber on top of things of his/her TV viewing expenses. There area unit a considerable range of subscribers UN agency pay a monthly charge, except for some reason or another area unit unable to look at TV on a day to day. Tata Skys Daily recharge currently permits them to currently select once to procure their TV viewing. For an oversized a part of the population, they'll economize and re-charge their set prime box on days once electricity is out there, or after they area unit back from vacation. Similarly, they'll prefer days once to not recharge examinationple|for instance|as an example} throughout exam days or once motion aloof from home.
                 </span>
                 <br/>
                 <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                  <br/>
                 </span>
                 <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                  "Commenting on the revolutionary concept, Mr. Harit Nagpal, MD &amp; CEO, Tata Sky, said: We are confident that the introduction of Tata Skys Daily Recharge will gain traction across the nation. The Daily Recharge option available at Rs. 8, 10, 20, 50 and 100 enables us to put power in the consumers hands to choose their level of convenience. It also elevates the DTH sector by redefining the pace of digitization and reach to markets nationwide.
                 </span>
                 <br/>
                 <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                  <br/>
                 </span>
                 <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                  With the understanding that there's a requirement in smaller cities and villages for bite sized consumption (much like shampoo sachets and tiny sized mobile recharges), the Daily Recharge card permits Tata Sky to create inroads into these untapped markets. Moreover, with conversion clinical trial still a year away, this set up ought to facilitate accelerate acceptance of DTH sector in Asian country.
                 </span>
                 <br/>
                 <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                  <br/>
                 </span>
                 <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                  How it works: Tata sky Subscriber  conceive to watch TV =&gt; Purchase the Daily Recharge card from a close-by store =&gt; Scratch and SMS {the range|the amount|the quantity} given from a registered mobile number =&gt; fancy tv viewing for the day.
                 </span>
                 <div style="clear: both;">
                 </div>
                </div>
